# Account in Financial

Business that represents a customer or potential customer. The company that is billed in business transactions.  
  
 Latest version of the JSON entity definition is available on <a href="https://github.com/Microsoft/CDM/tree/master/schemaDocuments/Healthcare/Financial/Financial/Account.cdm.json" target="_blank">GitHub</a>.

|[createdByExternalParty](#createdByExternalParty)|Shows the external party who created the record.|<a href="Account.md" target="_blank">Financial/Account</a>|

|[SLAInvokedId](#SLAInvokedId)|Last SLA that was applied to this case. This field is for internal use only.|<a href="Account.md" target="_blank">Financial/Account</a>|
